SELECT "t"."Id", "t"."Content", "t"."CreatedAt", "t"."Excerpt", "t"."FeaturedImageId", "t"."IsFavourite", "t"."IsPublished", "t"."PostCategoryId", "t"."Slug", "t"."Title", "t"."UpdatedAt", "t"."ViewCount", "p0"."Id", "p0"."AltText", "p0"."FileExtension", "p0"."FileName", "p0"."FilePath", "p0"."FileSize", "p0"."UploadDate"
FROM (
    SELECT "p"."Id", "p"."Content", "p"."CreatedAt", "p"."Excerpt", "p"."FeaturedImageId", "p"."IsFavourite", "p"."IsPublished", "p"."PostCategoryId", "p"."Slug", "p"."Title", "p"."UpdatedAt", "p"."ViewCount"
    FROM "Posts" AS "p"
    ORDER BY "p"."CreatedAt" DESC
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS "t"
LEFT JOIN "PostImages" AS "p0" ON "t"."FeaturedImageId" = "p0"."Id"
ORDER BY "t"."CreatedAt" DESC
